our top pick for most people, while the Samsung Galaxy S21 is best for Android fans. </strong></li>\n</ul><p>You can&#39;t go wrong with any of the major flagship smartphones that have been released in 2020 and 2021 so far. You can even get excellent phones for under $500 or less these days.</p><p>In this guide, we&#39;ve selected the absolute best phones we&#39;d recommend to the vast majority of people. We&#39;re also recommending the best phones for Android users, photography, battery life, gaming, kids, and the best phone for less.</p><p>Worthy of note, Apple recently announced its new <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/iphone-13-release-date-price-preorder-2021-9\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">iPhone 13 series</a>. We can&#39;t officially say that the new iPhone 13 is the best overall phone you can buy at the moment, as we haven&#39;t tested it yet. With that said, we&#39;re confident that it will comfortably replace the iPhone 12 as the best overall phone you can buy, based on experience.</p><h2>Here are the best phones:</h2><ul overall\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f85fb1791aa9e001880b65d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Apple iPhone 12\" height=\"1470\" width=\"1960\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Apple</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>The easiest smartphone to recommend to almost anyone is Apple's <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fbuy-iphone%2Fiphone-12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">iPhone 12</a>. It has the best overall combination of price, design, screen quality, performance, features, battery life, longevity, and camera quality out of any smartphone. But it will likely be replaced by the iPhone 13 as the top phone soon. </strong></p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Premium design, excellent performance, fantastic camera quality, Apple's ecosystem</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Charger not included, still uses Lightning instead of USB-C for charging, 60Hz iPhone screen is not as smooth and fluid as Android rivals' 90Hz or 120Hz screens</p><p>On its own, the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fbuy-iphone%2Fiphone-12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">iPhone 12</a> isn't much more special than Android alternatives that also come with top specs and features. The reasons why the iPhone 12 series in general places above Android alternatives as the top overall smartphone is mostly due to the magnificent Apple ecosystem, including AirPods, Apple Watch, iPad, and Mac computers that connect with each other seamlessly to offer useful features. More unique to Apple is the company's physical presence with its stores that gives users a clear place to go for support.</p><p>Another major reason for recommending the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fbuy-iphone%2Fiphone-12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">iPhone 12</a> series over Android alternatives is the timely iOS operating system updates that Apple delivers, and iPhones are supported for longer than any Android rival.&#160;</p><p>For most people, we recommend the standard $800 <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fbuy-iphone%2Fiphone-12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">iPhone 12</a> for its value and core feature set rather than the Pro series that start at $1,000. Most importantly, both phones share the same A14 processor, so they have similar performance, if not identical, for running apps and iOS. The extra features you get in the iPhone 12 Pro series mostly focus on enhanced camera hardware and software, like an extra camera lens for zoom, a LiDar scanner for better portrait mode shots in low light, and the Pro RAW mode for finer editing capabilities. Those are great, but aren't necessary for the complete iPhone experience that the iPhone 12 delivers, especially for the Pro series' $200 premium.&#160;&#160;</p><p>And, for those who prefer smaller phones for one-handed usability, the $700 iPhone 12 Mini with a 5.4-inch screen is an ideal alternative.</p><p>Apple still sells the iPhone 12 for $100 less than its $800 launch price after the company announced the iPhone 13. It's still a great phone to buy today, but you may want to hold off on buying a new iPhone until reviews for the iPhone 13 come out.</p>\n\tThe best Android phone\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60006804a8de7700187d3d72?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Samsung Galaxy S21 pink\" height=\"1318\" width=\"1760\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Samsung</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Samsung's <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545199829300418\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21</a> proves to be the best Android phone you can buy so far in 2021. It has the best balance of design, performance, features, camera versatility and quality, and price than any other Android smartphone.</strong></p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> Premium design, latest specs and highest performance on Android, triple-lens camera system, reduced pricing compared to last year's generation</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Photos can have an overly processed look, doesn't support Samsung's full 45W charging, 25W charger not included</p><p>Indeed, inside the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545199829300418\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21</a> is the latest Qualcomm Snapdragon 888 processor that delivers fast performance. Combined with 8GB of memory (RAM), the Galaxy S21 can easily handle workloads from users who often use and switch between lots of different apps without reloading.</p><p>The <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545199829300418\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21</a> also has Samsung's signature best-in-class display with vibrant colors, dynamic contrast, and incredible brightness. It's a 120Hz refresh rate screen at 1080p resolution, which makes for an ultra-smooth and premium experience while navigating around Android and swiping around apps. At 6.1-inches, the screen and overall size of the Galaxy S21 is best suited for those who like mid-sized phones, as on-screen items are still reachable with your thumbs if you prefer smaller phones that can be used one-handed. If you like larger phones, the Galaxy S21 Plus and its 6.7-inch screen will suit nicely.&#160;</p><p>The triple-lens camera system on the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545199829300418\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21</a> offers a 12-megapixel (MP) standard wide lens, a 12MP ultra-wide lens with 120-degrees field-of-view, and a 64MP 3x hybrid zoom lens that can go all the way up to 30x digital zoom. Camera quality is as expected from Samsung &#8212; that's to say you'll get beautiful photos if you don't mind the occasional over-processed look that can make them appear pre-enhanced. If you have experience with Samsung phones and you've liked the photos they produce, you won't have any issues here. However, if you prefer less processing on your photos, your best bet on Android is going to be Google's Pixel 5.&#160;</p><p>You get a big 4,000mAh battery in the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545199829300418\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21</a> that will last a full day of varied usage. It can charge at speeds up to 25W, which is fast enough, but Samsung unfortunately has not included a 25W charger with the phone. That means your older charger from your older phone may not charge the Galaxy S21 at its full capable speeds, and you'll have to buy your own charger. It does not support Samsung's 45W charger, either.&#160;</p><p>Back to positive news, Samsung dropped the price tag down $200 compared to its previous generation of Galaxy S20 devices, making the Galaxy S21's $800 price tag much more reasonable in the premium Android phone category. That's still expensive, but <a href=\"https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-raises-the-bar-for-mobile-experience-innovation-committing-to-three-generations-of-android-os-upgrades\">Samsung announced</a> in August 2020 that it promises to update Android on some of its Galaxy phones for up to three generations of Android. That extends the relevance of the Galaxy S21, as well as the usable lifespan of the device should users want to stay up to date with the latest versions of Android.&#160;</p>\n\tThe best phone for photography\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/600067eba8de7700187d3d6e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Samsung Galaxy S21 Ultra back\" height=\"1339\" width=\"1786\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Samsung</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Samsung's <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545235880730320\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21 Ultra</a> is the best phone for photography, and that's largely due to the sheer versatility that its quad-camera lens system has to offer.&#160;</strong></p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> Widest range of camera lenses, 108-megapixel sensor makes for ultra-detailed photos, best zooming in any phone, 4K and 8K video recording, \"pro\" mode and and RAW, useful video recording features</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Photos can appear overly processed at times</p><p>Indeed, the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545235880730320\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21 Ultra</a> has a 108MP standard wide lens, a 12MP ultra-wide lens, a 10MP 3x zoom lens, and a 10x zoom lens that can digitally zoom all the way up to 100x zoom.&#160;</p><p>To be sure, the iPhone 12 Pro Max takes great photos that are arguably better than the Galaxy S21 Ultra's, which can seem overly processed at times, but it can't compete against the Galaxy S21 Ultra's specs or versatility.</p><p>The 108MP standard lens on the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545235880730320\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21 Ultra</a> actually takes 12MP photos by default, but users can quickly switch on the 108MP mode that captures more detail. That extra detail becomes apparent when you zoom into a 108MP photo.&#160;</p><p>The Galaxy S21 Ultra also has superior zooming capabilities over any other phone we know about. By having two zoom lenses at different magnifications, the Galaxy S21 Ultra can take clear and detailed zoomed photos at a wider range of distance.</p><p>But, don't swoon over the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545235880730320\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21 Ultra</a>'s 100x ability &#8212; zooming at such distances produces bad, blurry photos with little value. Rather, we've found that zooming up to 30x digital zoom is the limit before photos start to actively look bad. Still, that's more zoom than other phones have to offer.</p><p>To top it all off, the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730545235880730320\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Galaxy S21 Ultra</a> can record video at 4K at 30fps, 4K at 60fps, and even 8K at 24fps. There are some genuinely useful video recording features here, like the new Director's View mode lets you see what all the camera lenses see, and you can seamlessly switch between each lens, even while recording. You can also record from a rear lens and selfie camera simultaneously.</p>\n\tThe best phone for battery life\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60108fa76dfbe10018e0021e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Motorola Moto G\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Best Buy</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>If battery life matters above all else, Motorola's <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730546336088412381\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Moto G Power</a> is the undisputed choice for its extremely long three-day battery life and its excellent value in relation to its performance, camera quality, and design.</strong></p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> The longest battery life, solid performance, incredible value, large 6.6-inch screen, good camera</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Included charger is slow, no frills or premium features (not expected)</p><p>You get a lot of phone for the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730546336088412381\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Moto G Power</a>'s starting price of $200 &#8212; apart from its huge battery life, the capable and power-efficient Qualcomm Snapdragon 662 can run almost any app that more expensive phones can, albeit not quite as quickly. It also comes with a good camera, as well as a large, power-efficient 6.6-inch 720p resolution screen.&#160;&#160;</p><p>But, to maximize power efficiency, you're not getting a lot of frills or premium features, and that's the way it goes if you value battery life. You're not getting super high-resolution displays with high refresh rates, no 5G connectivity speeds, no wireless charging, no NFC for mobile contactless payments, no telephoto or ultra-wide camera lenses, and not the fastest processor. But, you are getting a great, basic core smartphone experience that has arguably all you really need in a smartphone.&#160;</p><p>Included with the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730546336088412381\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Moto G Power</a> is a 10W charger that's not especially fast, but the phone supports up to 15W charging speeds, if you happen to have a phone charger that outputs 15W or more.</p><p>While three days is the official claim, battery life will likely vary depending on what you do on the phone. If you play a lot of games, you'll surely experience less than three days. Same goes if you're a heavy user who keeps the screen on and runs apps all day. Still, no matter what you do on the <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1730546336088412381\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Moto G Power</a>, you're still going to get better battery life than any smartphone we know of.</p>\n\tThe best phone for gaming\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/601090a96dfbe10018e00226?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Asus Rog III\" height=\"900\" href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bhphotovideo.com%2Fc%2Fproduct%2F1585042-REG%2Fasus_zs661ks_12g512g_rog_phone_3_dual_sim.html%2FBI%2F20673%2FKBID%2F15977%2FDFF%2Fd10-v21-t1-x1063694%2FSID%2FEZ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Asus ROG III</a> comes with features that mobile gamers will appreciate, like its Air Trigger sensors on the top edge of the phone that act like controller-style shoulder buttons when you hold it horizontally.</strong></p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Air Trigger sensors for extra controls on games, offset USB-C charging port, high-end specs tuned for gaming, better cooling than most phones, huge battery, high refresh rate screen</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Phone is very large and heavy, cameras are lackluster, design isn't for everyone</p><p>Another of the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bhphotovideo.com%2Fc%2Fproduct%2F1585042-REG%2Fasus_zs661ks_12g512g_rog_phone_3_dual_sim.html%2FBI%2F20673%2FKBID%2F15977%2FDFF%2Fd10-v21-t1-x1063694%2FSID%2FEZ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Asus ROG III</a>'s thoughtful gaming-centric features is the offset USB-C charging port that makes it easier to hold the phone in horizontal mode without the charging cable getting in the way.&#160;</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bhphotovideo.com%2Fc%2Fproduct%2F1585042-REG%2Fasus_zs661ks_12g512g_rog_phone_3_dual_sim.html%2FBI%2F20673%2FKBID%2F15977%2FDFF%2Fd10-v21-t1-x1063694%2FSID%2FEZ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Asus ROG III</a> also comes with high-end specs for high gaming performance, including the Qualcomm Snapdragon 865+ that's tuned to run at slightly higher speeds than the standard Snapdragon 865. That extra power from the Snapdragon 865+ causes more heat, which normally leads to processors automatically slowing themselves down to prevent overheating, but Asus thought of that, and this is a gaming phone, afterall. Indeed, the ROG III has better cooling than most normal phones, and it comes with a cooling fan accessory that helps dissipate heat, too.&#160;</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bhphotovideo.com%2Fc%2Fproduct%2F1585042-REG%2Fasus_zs661ks_12g512g_rog_phone_3_dual_sim.html%2FBI%2F20673%2FKBID%2F15977%2FDFF%2Fd10-v21-t1-x1063694%2FSID%2FEZ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">ROG III</a>'s screen is also geared for gamers with its high 144Hz refresh rate for smooth visuals in games. It's a 1080p resolution display, which might seem low for such a high-end phone, but it's plenty sharp, and it helps with battery life, too.&#160;</p><p>Speaking of battery life, the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bhphotovideo.com%2Fc%2Fproduct%2F1585042-REG%2Fasus_zs661ks_12g512g_rog_phone_3_dual_sim.html%2FBI%2F20673%2FKBID%2F15977%2FDFF%2Fd10-v21-t1-x1063694%2FSID%2FEZ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">ROG III</a> has a massive 6,000mAh battery to help power the phone longer than most others while gaming. And, the included 30W charger makes for fast charging.</p>\n\tThe best phone for kids\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f22fbe32618b922bb74a15f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Pixel 4a front\" height=\"1107\" width=\"1476\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Antonio Villas-Boas/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>What phone you'd like to give your kids will largely depend on which ecosystem you &#8212; the parents or guardians &#8212; are entrenched in, whether it's Apple's iOS or Google's Android. It's also wise to get a durable case for the phone, whichever model you go for.</strong></p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Less expensive but still great smartphones, smaller overall size</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>A little expensive for younger kids</p><p>For kids, we're recommending smaller and less expensive phones. That way, they're easier to handle for younger kids, and the blow from kids' phones getting lost or broken will be less impactful. While these are less expensive phones, they're no duds, either. Getting a phone that's too underpowered means it won't last very long in terms of usability, and phones aren't like clothes &#8212; they last longer than growing kids' clothing.&#160;&#160;</p><p>It used to be the case that iPhones were too expensive to realistically suggest for kids, but the $400 iPhone SE changed that. While it's certainly still expensive, it's the cheapest and smallest iPhone that comes with recent specs to ensure longevity. It's the best option for parents or guardians who use iPhones, as they will be familiar with the iOS operating system, ecosystem, and it's easier to get accustomed with the parental controls that are built into iOS.&#160;</p><p>The <a href=\"https://mysupport.apple.com/add-coverage/producttypes\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">AppleCare+ for iPhone</a> extended warranty is also a good safety net to get for a kid's iPhone, seeing as you get two cheaper repairs up to twice a year and theft/loss coverage.</p><p>For Android families, your best bet is the $350 <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B08CFSZLQ4/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=bipgf_020618_best-smartphones-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B08CFSZLQ4&#38;linkId=651947bb21f697abb7abc796402ccbc2\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Google Pixel 4a</a> for familiarity with the Android operating system, built-in parental controls, as well as for its relatively low price, good performance, and small size. It has a great camera that punches above its price tag, to boot.&#160;</p><p>Google also offers its own extended warranty called <a href=\"https://store.google.com/us/magazine/preferred_care\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Google Preferred Care</a> that gives you up to two incidents of accidental damage.</p>\n\tThe best phone for less\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6130e35f9ef1e50018f96699?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Google Pixel 5a thumbnail 4x3\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2400\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Antonio Villas-Boas/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong><a href=\"https://store.google.com/us/product/pixel_5a_5g?hl=en-US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Google's Pixel 5a</a> is all the phone anyone ever needs. It's powerful </strong><strong><em>enough</em></strong><strong>, it has fantastic cameras, a nice screen, fantastic battery life, and it's priced at an affordable $450. It's a true \"phone for the people.\"</strong></p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Under $500, speedy for the price, great screen, excellent battery life, premium wide and ultra-wide cameras, headphone jack, 18W fast charger included, IP67 water resistance</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> No wireless charging</p><p>The <a href=\"https://store.google.com/us/product/pixel_5a_5g?hl=en-US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Pixel 5a</a> shows very clearly that spending more on premium phones offers rapidly diminishing returns. The performance gains from spending more are somewhat noticeable but hardly worth the extra hundreds. And you're not getting better cameras for the price. In fact, you're not getting better cameras by spending twice as much, either.</p><p>Phone users who are used to premium phones may have a hard time adjusting to the Pixel 5a. It's just a smidge less speedy and powerful, and it doesn't come with certain premium features like wireless charging or an ultra-premium metal and glass build. But unlike the expensive premium phones today, you <em>are</em> getting a fast charger included with the phone.&#160;</p><p>Otherwise, just about everything else in the <a href=\"https://store.google.com/us/product/pixel_5a_5g?hl=en-US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Pixel 5a</a>, including the cameras, the screen, the battery life, and peripheral features like water resistance, handily match phones that cost hundreds more.&#160;</p><p>You can read the full <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/google-pixel-5a-5g-review\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Google Pixel 5a 5G</a> review here to check out this marvel of a device in more detail.</p>\n\tWhat else we considered\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9088f8212113001873ffca?format=jpeg\" alt=\"pixel 5 1\" height=\"1178\" width=\"1571\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Antonio Villas-Boas/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>We have tested dozens of new phones over the past year to come up with our top picks. There are many other great options that we haven't included in our top four for various reasons. Here's what else we considered:</p><p><strong>OnePlus 9:</strong> The OnePlus 9 series are fine, powerful, and feature-rich phones, but they didn't quite make the cut. The cameras aren't quite up to snuff, which we could excuse if their price tags were lower.&#160;</p><p><strong>Google Pixel 5:</strong> We also considered Google's latest Pixel 5, and we recommend it for those looking for the best camera quality in any phone. With that said, the Pixel 5's good-but-mid-range Snapdragon 765G processor and performance doesn't pull its $700 weight, especially when other $700 phones come with higher specs.</p><p>But Pixel phones typically get new Android features before other phones, and that's continuing in 2021. Later this year, the Pixel will be getting first dibs on recently announced updates, including photography upgrades to help better capture skin color and curly hair, custom color palettes for apps based on your background photo, and a Cinematic Movement feature &#8211; which creates moving pictures across any of your photos. You can read the full <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/google-pixel-5-review\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Pixel 5 review</a> here.</p>\n\tWe look forward to testing these 2021 flagship phones as they launch\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6001fab4e3d62500185fcdee?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Galaxy S21, S21 Plus, S21 Ultra\" height=\"1889\" width=\"2519\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Samsung</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>We're looking forward to testing Apple's recently announced iPhone 13 models, and we're confident that it will replace the incumbent iPhone 12 as the best phone for most people to buy.&#160;</p><p>Later in the year, we're expecting the new Google Pixel 6, which promises a total refresh of Google's premium phone strategy. Android phone users should wait until Google announces the Pixel 6 before making any buying decisions on a new phone.</p>\n\tThere's only one foldable phone we recommend\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e4c2bdc3b62b775ac3d79b2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Galaxy Z Flip Open\" height=\"2477\" width=\"3302\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lisa Eadicicco/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>If you're desperate to buy a foldable phone, let it be Samsung's Galaxy Z Flip 3. It's the first foldable we'd recommend because, unlike previous foldables, it's priced relatively well for its specs.&#160;</p><p>The Galaxy Z Flip 3 is part of Samsung's third generation of foldable phones, and you can truly tell how far the company has come with its foldable screens and hinge technology. Overall, it really is a good phone, except for the battery life. movement.</p><p>FedEx said that the driver was no longer working for the company, but wouldn&#39;t say whether he quit or was fired. The driver said he quit.</p><p>In a <a href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/@vincentmrworldwid/video/7008670809149525254?lang=en&is_copy_url=1&is_from_webapp=v1ebapp=v1\">video posted September 16</a>, Vincent Paterno said he would also ignore houses that &#34;don&#39;t have a flag in front,&#34; seemingly a reference to the American flag. Paterno replied, &#34;medical supplies have priority no matter who you voted for.&#34;</p><p>Paterno was wearing a FedEx polo shirt in the video.</p><p>A spokesperson for FedEx told Insider the company was &#34;appalled by the behavior depicted in this video, which does not reflect the views of FedEx.&#34; </p><p>&#34;This individual is no longer providing service on behalf of the company,&#34; they said.</p><p><a href=\"https://news.yahoo.com/fedex-fires-driver-refused-deliver-205944592.html\">Some media outlets</a> reported that FedEx fired Paterno after the TikTok went viral. could get fired when I didn&#39;t work there anymore,&#34; he added.</p><p>When asked by Insider whether Paterno quit, the FedEx spokesperson said that the company &#34;[doesn&#39;t] discuss the 00:55:29","updatedTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:29","title":"The 20 best of the largest airports in the US, according to travelers","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/jd-power-reveals-top-mega-airport-in-terms-customer-satisfaction-2021-9","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614ce42a4c42bc00190fa7fb?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Miami International Airport\" height=\"724\" width=\"965\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Miami International Airport\n<p class=\"copyright\">mariakray/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>J.D. Power revealed Miami International Airport as the best mega airport in the US in terms of customer satisfaction.</li>\n<li>The study ranked airports based on six factors, like terminal facilities and vendor availability.</li>\n<li>The company says customer satisfaction decreased from January to July due to changing expectations among travelers.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>J.D. Power revealed its <a href=\"https://www.jdpower.com/business/press-releases/2021-north-america-airport-satisfaction-study\">2021 North America Airport Satisfaction Study</a> on Wednesday, naming Miami International Airport as the top mega airport in the US, earning 828 out of a possible 1,000 customer satisfaction points. The data analytics company looked at six factors in ranking each airport, including, from most to least important, terminal facilities; airport arrival/departure; baggage claim; security check; check-in/baggage check; and food, beverage, and retail.</p><p>Overall, mega airports, which J.D. Power defines as having more than 33 million passengers per year, received an average score of 798, up 18 points from 2020. This year saw a record-setting average score of 802 for all US airports, though the highest customer satisfaction occurred in the first half of the study (July 2020 to January 2021) when passenger traffic was still low and dropped in the second half (January 2021 to July 2021) as volume picked up. </p><p>&#34;Airport customer satisfaction reached all-time highs when passenger volumes were severely suppressed by the pandemic, but as leisure travel rebounded sharply throughout the spring and summer of 2021, we saw an expected downturn in satisfaction. Ultimately, the data conveys changing expectations among travelers. Early in the pandemic, passengers were satisfied with any shop or restaurant being open, but they now expect full service at the airport,&#34; explained Michael Taylor, travel intelligence lead at J.D. Power.</p><p>While passenger volumes have increased to 75% of pre-pandemic levels, according to J.D. Power, many travelers are arriving at airports with limited food, beverage, and retail options, which are key for a good airport experience. The company says <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/labor-shortage-wages-sign-on-bonus-airport-restaurants-poaching-workers-2021-6\">labor shortages are to blame for the lack of vendors</a>.</p><p>Here&#39;s a closer look at J.D. Power&#39;s top 20 airports for customer satisfaction in the US.</p><h2>20. Chicago O&#39;Hare International Airport: 772 points</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e386eb414c10018626247?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Chicago O&#39;Hare International Airport\" height=\"3024\" width=\"4032\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Chicago O&#39;Hare International Airport dropped one spot from 19 to 20 in this year&#39;s list. The airport is the city&#39;s largest and acts as a base for United Airlines and American Airlines and as a focus city for Frontier Airlines. Before becoming O&#39;Hare, <a href=\"https://chicago.curbed.com/2017/9/20/16338794/chicago-airport-travel-ohare-flights\">the land was used as an airfield for Douglas C-54 military production during WWII</a>, but after the closure of Douglas, the building was renamed Orchard Field Airport. O&#39;Hare&#39;s &#34;ORD&#34; IATA code is a homage to its original name.</p><h2>19. Toronto Pearson International Airport: 780 points</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614ce61e4c42bc00190fa8c1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Toronto airport\" height=\"3332\" width=\"4443\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.shutterstock.com/image-photo/toronto-canada-march-2nd-2018-modern-1050656627?src=nqvwHIF5hCNTLdAONQ4BCg-1-16\" target=\"_blank\">Shutterstock</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Toronto Pearson International Airport is the only Canadian airport to make the top 20 list, though it fell one spot from 18 in 2020 to 19 in 2021. <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/toronto-pearson-international-airport-yyz\">Toronto is the country&#39;s busiest airport</a> and has the largest terminal of any airport in Canada. It serves over 40 commercial, charter, and cargo airlines and is a hub for Air Canada, Sunwing Airlines, WestJet, FedEx Express, Air Georgian, and Air Transat.</p><h2>18. Boston Logan International Airport: 784 points</h2><h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614ce7ebde0e7b00194c1b9f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Boston Logan International Airport\" height=\"1664\" width=\"2218\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">JOSEPH PREZIOSO/AFP/Getty</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></h2><p>Boston Logan International Airport dropped six spots from 12 to 18 in this year&#39;s rankings. The airport is the <a href=\"https://www.tripsavvy.com/new-england-airports-4098163\">largest in New England in terms of passengers traffic and cargo handling</a> and the busiest in the Northeast behind the New York City metropolitan area. Boston is a hub for Delta Air Lines and Cape Air and is a focus city for JetBlue Airways.</p><h2>17. Seattle-Tacoma International Airport: 789 points</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3c4e2fb46b0019be1710?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Seattle Tacoma International Airport\" height=\"1000\" width=\"1333\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.shutterstock.com/image-photo/seattle-wa-27-june-2016-seatac-662230153?src=zafUHZpyMbz1H97uyvqDbg-1-1\" target=\"_blank\">EQRoy/Shutterstock</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Seattle-Tacoma International Airport fell one spot from 2020&#39;s list to 17. It is the <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/seattle-tacoma-international-airport-sea\">city&#39;s largest and primary commercial airport serving over 25 airlines</a> and an average of three million passengers per year. Seattle-Tacoma is one of the US&#39; fasting growing airports and is a hub for Alaska Airlines and Horizon Air.</p><h2>15. Newark Liberty International Airport: 792 points (tie)</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614ceac1de0e7b00194c1d55?format=jpeg\" alt=\"United Club Newark Airport\" height=\"1665\" width=\"2221\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Terminal C at Newark Liberty International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Newark Liberty International Airport jumped five spots to 15 this year, tieing with Los Angeles International Airport. <a href=\"https://www.contienterprises.com/index.php/projects/newark-airport-terminal-b-bridges-and-pump-stations#:~:text=As%20America's%20oldest%20airfield%20and,New%20York%20City%20metropolitan%20area.rea.\">Newark is the country&#39;s oldest airfield</a>, having opened in 1928, and home to America&#39;s first commercial terminal. Today, the airport serves over 30 airlines and is a hub for United Airlines and FedEx Express.<a href=\"https://www.contienterprises.com/index.php/projects/newark-airport-terminal-b-bridges-and-pump-stations#:~:text=As%20America's%20oldest%20airfield%20and,New%20York%20City%20metropolitan%20area.rea.\"></a></p><h2>15. Los Angeles International Airport: 792 points (tie)</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614dfeefb414c10018624cba?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Los Angeles International Airport\" height=\"722\" width=\"962\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Los Angeles International Airport\n<p class=\"copyright\">OLOS/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Los Angeles International Airport tied with Newark Liberty International Airport for its number 15 spot, up to two from 2020. The airport is the <a href=\"https://www.lawa.org/history/lax-history/just-the-facts\">second busiest airport in the US</a> and the fourth busiest in the world serving over 69 airlines. Los Angeles is a <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/los-angeles-international-airport-lax\">hub for Alaska, United, Delta, American, and Southwest</a>, and is a focus city for Allegiant and JetBlue.</p><h2>13. Fort Lauderdale-Hollywood International Airport: 793 points (tie)</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e39752fb46b0019be15b9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Fort Lauderdale-Hollywood International Airport\" height=\"724\" width=\"965\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Fort Lauderdale-Hollywood International Airport\n<p class=\"copyright\">YES Market Media/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Fort Lauderdale-Hollywood International Airport tied with Denver International Airport in this year&#39;s rankings, jumping from the number 13 spot in 2020 and expanding from a large to a mega airport in 2021. Fort Lauderdale is <a href=\"https://www.fort-lauderdale-airport.com/\">one of Florida&#39;s busiest airports carrying over 36 million passengers in 2019</a>. The airport serves 19 airlines and is a <a href=\"https://www.flightconnections.com/flights-from-fort-lauderdale-fll\">hub for Silver Airways and Spirit Airlines</a> and is a focus city for JetBlue and Allegiant.</p><h2>13. Denver International Airport: 793 points (tie)</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e39a0b414c100186262f9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Denver International Airport\" height=\"2142\" width=\"2857\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">JW_PNW/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Denver International Airport tied with Fort Lauderdale-Hollywood International Airport, dropping from spot number five to 13 in 2021. <a href=\"https://www.flydenver.com/about\">Denver is the fifth busiest airport in the US and 20th busiest in the world</a>, having handled 69 million passengers in 2019. The airport is the US&#39; largest airport in terms of size and serves as a hub for United and Frontier.</p><h2>11. San Francisco International Airport: 796 points (tie)</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e39ebb414c10018626330?format=jpeg\" alt=\"10 san francisco international airport\" height=\"3744\" width=\"4992\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">San Francisco International Airport</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>San Francisco International Airport tied with Charlotte Douglas International Airport in this year&#39;s rankings, jumping four spots. The airport is the <a href=\"https://www.flysfo.com/sfo-fact-sheet\">second busiest in California after Los Angeles</a> and hosts 59 airlines serving dozens of international and domestic markets. San Francisco is a <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/san-francisco-international-airport-sfo\">hub for United and Alaska</a>.</p><h2>11. Charlotte Douglas International Airport: 796 points (tie)</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6126abd9e4235b00180a8e6e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Charlotte Douglas International Airport.\" height=\"2711\" width=\"3615\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Charlotte Douglas International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Fang Deng/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Charlotte Douglas International Airport tied with San Francisco International Airport at number 11, jumping one spot from 2020. Charlotte is the <a href=\"https://charlotteregion.com/eco-dev/airport-fast-facts/\">12th busiest airport in North America</a> by passenger traffic, handling nearly 50 million travelers per year. The airport hosts over 30 airlines and is a <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/charlotte-douglas-international-airport-clt\">hub for American Airlines</a>.</p><h2>9. Hartsfield-Jackson Atlanta International Airport: 798 points (tie)</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3a87b414c10018626381?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Hartsfield Jackson\" height=\"2000\" width=\"2666\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The main hall inside Hartsfield-Jackson Atlanta International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.shutterstock.com/image-photo/atlanta-georgia-july-27-2015-main-317731922?src=SVGVfFn94djrJkS6uxg2eQ-1-2\" target=\"_blank\">ESBProfessional/shutterstock</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Hartsfield-Jackson Atlanta International Airport ranked number nine this year, jumping up one spot and tieing with Detroit Metropolitan Airport. <a href=\"https://www.amaconferencecenters.org/atlantas-hartsfield-jackson-international-facts-about-the-worlds-busiest-airport/\">Atlanta is within a two-hour flight of 80% of the US population</a> and handled over 100 million travelers in 2019. The airport serves over 30 airlines and is the primary <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/atlanta-hartsfield-jackson-international-airport-atl\">hub for Delta Air Lines</a>. The airport held the title of the world&#39;s busiest airport for years, but the pandemic plummeted its passenger traffic in 2020. </p><h2>9. Detroit Metropolitan Airport: 798 points (tie)</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3ab2b414c10018626394?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Detroit Metropolitan Airport\" height=\"664\" width=\"886\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Detroit Metropolitan Airport\n<p class=\"copyright\">afrimu/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Detroit Metropolitan Airport tied with Hartsfield-Jackson Atlanta International Airport to take the number nine spot this year, dropping two spots from number seven in 2020. Detroit sees over <a href=\"https://www.metroairport.com/about-dtw\">36 million passengers per year</a> and serves more than 25 airlines. The airport is a hub for <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/detroit-metropolitan-airport-dtw\">Delta Air Lines and Spirit Airlines</a>.</p><h2>8. George Bush Intercontinental Airport: 801 points</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3aeb2fb46b0019be1660?format=jpeg\" alt=\"George bush\" height=\"2000\" width=\"2666\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>View of George Bush Intercontinental Airport Terminal E at night\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.shutterstock.com/image-photo/houston-tx-january-14-2018-view-796036942?src=8-sISUQLCd8W4jLMZ3kbaQ-1-3\" target=\"_blank\">Eblis/shutterstock</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>George Bush Intercontinental Airport ranked eighth this year after not making the top 20 list last year. Named after the 41st president, George Bush airport <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/houston-george-bush-intercontinental-airport-iah\">hosts over 30 airlines</a> and acts as a hub for Atlas Air and United Airlines. <a href=\"https://www.airport-houston.com/\">Houston serves over 30 markets in Mexico</a>, which is more than any other airport in the US. </p><h2>7. Dallas/Fort Worth International Airport: 805 points</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3b0a2fb46b0019be166f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Dallas/Fort Worth International Airport\" height=\"2000\" width=\"2666\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Taesik Park/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Dallas/Fort Worth International Airport ranked seven this year, dropping two spots from number five in 2020. The airport hosts over 25 airlines and is the <a href=\"https://www.dfwairport.com/business/about/facts/\">second-largest airport in terms of area size</a> behind Denver International Airport. Dallas is <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/dallas-fort-worth-international-airport-dfw\">American Airlines&#39; primary operating hub</a> and is a key transfer point for US-Latin America travelers.</p><h2>6. McCarran International Airport: 806 points</h2><h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3b23b414c100186263c6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"McCarran International Airport\" height=\"724\" width=\"965\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>McCarran International Airport\n<p class=\"copyright\">Tupungato/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></h2><p>McCarran International Airport dropped three spots from three to six in 2021&#39;s top 20 list. McCarran is Las Vegas&#39; primary airport <a href=\"https://www.las-vegas-airport.com/\">handling over 50 million passengers</a> in 2019. The airport hosts over 20 airlines and is a focus city for Allegiant Air, Frontier Airlines, JSX, Southwest Airlines, Spirit Airlines, and Sun Country Airlines. McCarran is one of only two airports in the US <a href=\"https://thepointsguy.com/news/ka-ching-tourist-ends-vegas-trip-by-hitting-300k-jackpot-at-airport-slot-machine/\">that have slot machines</a>, the other being Reno-Tahoe International Airport.</p><h2>5. Phoenix Sky Harbor International Airport: 808 points</h2><h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3b51b414c100186263de?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Phoenix Sky Harbor International Airport\" height=\"724\" width=\"965\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Phoenix Sky Harbor International Airport\n<p class=\"copyright\">Markus Mainka/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></h2><p>Phoenix Sky Harbor International Airport was the top airport in J.D. Power&#39;s 2020 list but dropped to number five this year. Sky Harbor is known as the <a href=\"https://www.azfamily.com/shows/good_morning_arizona/field_trip_friday/fun-facts-about-phoenix-sky-harbor-airport/article_b8d375f2-9981-11e9-b15b-9b44af1cbc2f.html\">friendliest airport in the US</a>, with 400 volunteers helping travelers navigate the airport. It serves more than 45 million passengers a year and is a major <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/phoenix-sky-harbor-international-airport-phx\">hub for American Airlines</a>.</p><h2>4. Orlando International Airport: 812 points</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3b87b414c100186263f3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Orlando International Airport\" height=\"966\" width=\"1289\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.shutterstock.com/image-photo/orlando-december-30-interior-atrium-international-92237335?src=8Rk5YKZEdpgx5_IprDnl6w-1-2\" target=\"_blank\">Sean Pavone/Shutterstock</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Orlando International Airport jumped two spots from six in 2020 to four in 2021. The airport is the second-busiest in Florida serving over 50 million passengers in 2019, though it <a href=\"https://thepointsguy.com/airport/mco/\">does not serve as a hub for any airline</a>. However, it is a focus city for Frontier Airlines, JetBlue Airways, Southwest Airlines, and Spirit Airlines. <a href=\"https://orlandoairports.net/faq/\">Orlando&#39;s IATA code &#34;MCO&#34;</a> comes from McCoy Air Force Base, named after Colonel Michael N. W. McCoy, which is what sat on the land before the airport was built.</p><h2>3. Minneapolis−Saint Paul International Airport: 815 points</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e1a2b2fb46b0019be08d7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Minneapolis Airport\" height=\"2000\" width=\"2666\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The atrium at Minneapolis-Saint Paul International Airport\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.shutterstock.com/image-photo/minneapolis-mn-july-02-airport-on-145640200?src=JXTF_epLcd7sIF4O6krTCg-1-2\" target=\"_blank\">Jeffrey J. Coleman/shutterstock</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Minneapolis−Saint Paul International Airport jumped four spots to number three in this year&#39;s rankings. The airport is nestled among a few cities in Minnesota, including Minneapolis, St. Paul, Bloomington, and Eagan, and is the busiest airport in the upper Midwest region. Minneapolis-St. Paul <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/minneapolis-st-paul-international-airport-msp\">serves over 25 airlines</a> and acts as a hub for Sun Country Airlines and Delta Air Lines.</p><h2>2. John F. Kennedy International Airport: 817 points</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3bd62fb46b0019be16ce?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Travel\" height=\"800\" width=\"1066\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>John F. Kennedy International Airport, New York.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Spencer Platt/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>New York&#39;s John F. Kennedy International Airport is this year&#39;s runner-up, jumping two spots from 2020. Named after the 35th president, JFK airport is a major international gateway serving over <a href=\"https://www.iflya380.com/fly-smart/five-fun-facts-about-John-F-Kennedy-international-airport-new-york.html?origin=HVN\">60 million passengers in 2019</a> and operating flights to all six inhabited continents. JFK is a <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/new-york-john-f-kennedy-international-airport-jfk\">hub for JetBlue Airways</a>, American Airlines, and Delta Air Lines.</p><h2>1. Miami International Airport: 828 points</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3bf7b414c10018626441?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Miami International Airport\" height=\"724\" width=\"965\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Miami International Airport\n<p class=\"copyright\">mariakray/Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Miami International Airport took the number one spot in the 2021 J.D. Power top 20 rankings, jumping one spot from 2020. The airport is the <a href=\"https://www.miami-airport.com/about_us.asp\">US&#39; third-busiest airport</a> in terms of passenger traffic and offers more flights to the Caribbean and Latin America than any other airport in the country. Miami is the top airport for cargo and hosts over 100 air carriers serving more than 140 destinations worldwide. The airport is a <a href=\"https://centreforaviation.com/data/profiles/airports/miami-international-airport-mia\">hub for American Airlines</a>, FedEx Express, LAN Cargo, and UPS Airlines, and its a focus city for Frontier Airlines, Avianca, and LATAM.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 00:55:29","updatedTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:29","title":"Google begins courtroom battle with EU in bid to quash record $5 billion fine over Android dominance","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/google-faces-eu-in-court-over-5-billion-android-fine-2021-9","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5c9201b5f73f5c34f8343005?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Sundar Pichai and Margrethe Vestager\" height=\"975\" width=\"1300\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Google CEO Sundar Pichai and Margrethe Vestager, the European competition commissioner.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Google has begun a five-day court battle with the EU over a $5 billion fine issued in 2018.</li>\n<li>Lawmakers say Google used Android&#39;s dominance to push its own apps and services. </li>\n<li>The company is facing mounting antitrust pressure in both the EU and the US. </li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Google has entered a five-day court battle with the European Union, as the tech giant seeks to overturn a $5 billion antitrust fine issued by the bloc in 2018. </p><p>The EU fined the tech giant over allegations of anti-competitive behavior - involving shopping, Android, and search advertising - three times in as many years: first <a href=\"https://www.reuters.com/article/us-eu-google-antitrust/eu-fines-google-record-2-7-billion-in-first-antitrust-case-idUSKBN19I108\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"40\" data-uri=\"e1a7c4befdfe2347fdba57dd9f5197fd\">for $2.7 billion in 2017</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/google-fined-by-eu-android-2018-7?r=US&IR=TIR=T\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"40\" data-uri=\"f69d5008e2cebc79ce5b2126e75ba105\">again for $5 billion in 2018</a>, and once more <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/google-fined-17-billion-for-breaking-eu-antitrust-rules-over-adsense-2019-3?r=US&IR=TIR=T\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"40\" data-uri=\"bd15215e787282e484e61a59559e5e18\">for $1.7 billion in 2019</a>.</p><p>In the second case, European competition authorities accused Google of abusing its dominant Android mobile operating system to cement the popularity of its own apps and services.</p><p>The bloc said Google had forced phone makers to preinstall its Chrome browser and its Search app as a condition for accessing the Play App Store.</p><p>Lawmakers also accused the company of illegally paying manufacturers to preinstall its Search app exclusively, protecting its search business from competition, and preventing Android phone makers from selling devices that run &#34;forked&#34; versions of the operating system. Google has repeatedly denied the commission&#39;s findings.</p><p>The company&#39;s lawyers will be seeking to overturn the bloc&#39;s record $5 billion levy this week at the EU&#39;s General Court in Luxembourg. The court is used to hear cases against the institutions of the EU.</p><p>&#34;Android has created more choice for everyone, not less, and supports thousands of successful businesses in Europe and around the world,&#34; a Google spokesman said. &#34;This case isn&#39;t supported by the facts or the law.&#34;</p><p>In a 2018 <a href=\"https://www.blog.google/around-the-globe/google-europe/android-has-created-more-choice-not-less/\">blog post</a> reacting to the $5 billion fine, Google CEO Sundar Pichai argued that the current Android system had &#34;created more choice, not less&#34; through its business practices, and that the EU&#39;s decision risked upsetting &#34;the careful balance that we have struck with Android.&#34; </p><p>&#34;Today&#39;s decision rejects the business model that supports Android, which has created more choice for everyone, not less,&#34; Pichai wrote at the time.</p><p>Google faces mounting antitrust pressure on either side of the Atlantic, with attorney generals from 36 US states, and Washington DC, recently <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/google-faces-nationwide-antitrust-lawsuit-over-android-app-store-2021-7?r=US&IR=TIR=T\">lodging a complaint</a> over the firm&#39;s control of the Android app store. </p><p>Insider approached the European Commission for comment. </p><p><em>Are you a current or former Google employee with more to share? href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">iPad Pro</a> beats Surface Pro 7 out on hardware, but is a far better tablet than it is a laptop.</li>\n<li aria-level=\"1\">Both 2-in-1 devices have their merits, but Surface Pro 7 is cheaper and works better as a laptop.</li>\n</ul><bi-shortcode id=\"table-of-contents-sticky\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-type=\"h2\">Table of Contents: Masthead Sticky</bi-shortcode><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"6086d988a3247900115896a3\" data-purchase-option=\"\">11-inch iPad Pro (2021) (small)</bi-shortcode><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"609ad2a6f3902d00118a7850\" data-purchase-option=\"\">12.9-inch iPad Pro (2021) (small)</bi-shortcode><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"5d962cb1625ac924a32238e8\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Surface Pro 7 (small)</bi-shortcode><p>Apple&#39;s iPad Pro has been encroaching on laptop territory since its introduction. Meanwhile, Microsoft&#39;s Surface Pro 2-in-1 detachable laptops have offered a laptop that could double as a tablet while running Windows for years. The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-ipad-pro-review-m1-2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">iPad Pro (M1)</a> is brand-new for 2021, and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/microsoft-surface-pro-7-review\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Surface Pro 7</a> just got a major price cut, so it&#39;s important for anyone on the market to know how they stack up.</p><p>This is especially true now considering that the Surface Pro 8 has been announced, which has seen the previous Surface Pro 7 price drop to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">as low as $549 already on Microsoft&#39;s online store</a>. This makes for an interesting comparison considering you could get a complete Surface Pro 7 package with a keyboard for much less than the latest iPad Pro.</p><h2>Microsoft Surface Pro 7 vs. Apple iPad Pro: Which is best?</h2><p>If you know you need the flexibility of the Windows operating system, there&#39;s no getting around that. Apple&#39;s iPadOS is just a little more locked down and may not support all the software you need. It also doesn&#39;t behave at all like the laptop&#39;s you might be used to, though iPadOS keeps getting better in that regard.</p><p>But, if your needs are more flexible, the Apple iPad Pro doesn&#39;t give the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Surface Pro 7</a> much room to shine. The Apple <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">iPad Pro</a> received a significant update this year that sets it ahead of the Surface Pro 7 (which came in late 2019) in almost all regards. Even the base model of the iPad Pro features enough performance to challenge even the most expensive Surface Pro 7 model. The iPad Pro display is also far better geared up for HDR content consumption. </p><table style=\"border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; height: 220px;\" border=\"1\"><tbody><tr style=\"height: 22px;\"><td style=\"width: 33.3333%; This is the same beastly System-on-Chip (SoC) seen in Apple&#39;s most recent <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-macbook-air-m1-vs-macbook-pro-m1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">MacBook Air and MacBook Pro</a>, and it&#39;s a performance champ. Most models come with 8GB of RAM, though the 1TB and 2TB models bump up to 16GB of RAM.</p><p>Meanwhile, the performance you&#39;ll get out of the Surface Pro 7 depends majorly on which model you buy. The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Surface Pro 7</a> starts with a humble, 10th-Gen Intel Core i3 dual-core processor and 4GB of RAM that will struggle with much beyond the basics. Microsoft offers versions packing Intel Core i7-1065G7 processors alongside 16GB of RAM that can run much faster (and even a Core i7-1165G7 model in the business-oriented Surface Pro 7+). </p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e2efe2fb46b0019be10b2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Apple’s 2021 iPad Pro has the new M1 chip\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The iPad Pro acts more like a tablet than the Surface Pro 7 because it runs on iPad OS and mobile apps.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lisa Eadicicco/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><p>Comparing base models, the iPad Pro&#39;s M1 chip with 8GB of RAM is all but guaranteed to blow the dated, 10th-Gen Intel Core i3 out of the water. The higher-end Surface Pro 7 models can keep better pace with the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">iPad Pro</a>, but Apple has a class-leading chip on its hands with the M1, and the Surface Pro 7 models just won&#39;t keep up when really pushed. </p><p>That said, the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Surface Pro 7</a> runs a full Windows operating system with all the versatility that allows, such as more direct file management, customizing your home screen, and downloading apps and files freely through a web browser or other sources.</p><p>Since iPadOS is more locked down, you may find fewer occasions to actually push the M1 chip to its limits. The extra performance in a higher-end Surface Pro 7 may help with future-proofing, but both machines will offer a zippy experience in most general workloads - excluding the Core i3 model.</p><h2>Battery life and features</h2><p>The Surface Pro 7 and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">iPad Pro</a> are both boasting similar battery life. Each tout something in the 10-hour ballpark, which could see either take the lead in real-world use. What separates the two devices more is their features. This division comes down more to their operating systems than anything else, though.</p><p>Both the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Surface Pro 7</a> and iPad Pro function as standalone tablets, though we&#39;d argue the iPad Pro is better suited in that role. They each have displays that support active styluses with pressure sensitivity, tilt, and palm rejection. These make both devices suited for drafting, drawing, and note-taking.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e2f8cb414c10018625e61?format=jpeg\" alt=\"surface pro 7 2019\" height=\"1500\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Surface Pro 7 is a better computer than it is a tablet, as the Windows OS and the apps it runs aren&#39;t especially well designed for touch input.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Antonio Villas-Boas/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><p>Both devices support attachable keyboard covers and trackpads or mice for navigation. That said, iPadOS has only recently gained support for mice as a replacement for touch inputs, and the interactions may feel clunky for anyone more used to a conventional mouse or trackpad on Mac or PC. By contrast, despite Windows having supported touch input for years, the operating system still feels poorly designed for the navigation method.</p><p>Apple comes out ahead in terms of cameras, especially considering the inclusion of a second rear camera and even a LiDAR sensor on the 12.9-inch model. Both devices offer comparable face recognition unlock methods with their front cameras, though. </p><p>Microsoft turns it around in flexibility, though. The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Surface Pro 7</a> offers more ports, including USB-A (standard USB), USB-C, a headphone jack, and even a microSD card port, to connect with various accessories. Meanwhile, the iPad Pro has a single USB-C port.</p><h2>Design and display</h2><p>The Surface Pro 7 is a bit dated next to the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">iPad Pro</a>, and that leaves a lot going in favor of Apple&#39;s tablet. </p><p>Apple can pack in a 12.9-inch display into a frame that&#39;s less than 3 square inches larger than the Surface Pro 7, which has a 12.3-inch display.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e2fe82fb46b0019be1102?format=jpeg\" alt=\"a woman in a blue shirt stands at a table of iPad Pros\" height=\"3600\" width=\"4800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The iPad Pro benefits from incredible performance compared to lower tier Surface Pro 7 models.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Mark Lennihan/Associated Press</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><p>Though both devices offer very sharp resolutions, Apple is also offering a better display. Microsoft&#39;s <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Surface Pro 7</a> screen can&#39;t get nearly as bright as either iPad Pro&#39;s, especially the iPad Pro 12.9&#39;s Mini LED display, which can hit up to 1,600 nits. HDR on the iPad Pro also benefits from these display upgrades, making Apple&#39;s device the better choice for consuming content.</p><p>You&#39;ll find premium metal frames on both devices, but Microsoft does benefit from its prioritization of laptop use cases. Where the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">iPad Pro</a> is just a tablet you can pair with a keyboard case, the Surface Pro 7 is more like a laptop that just doesn&#39;t include a keyboard, and laptops are meant to be stood upright. So, Microsoft&#39;s inclusion of a quality kickstand on the Surface Pro 7 makes it easy to set up for hands-free viewing or to use with any Bluetooth keyboard under the sun without needing a separate stand to hold the tablet up - no such luck with the iPad Pro. </p><h2>Operating system and apps</h2><p>The differences between the operating systems and app ecosystems of <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-announces-ipados-software-operating-system-for-ipad-wwdc-2019-6\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">iPadOS</a> and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/windows-10-review-2015-7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Windows 10</a> are extensive and can&#39;t be covered comprehensively here, but we&#39;ll provide an overview. Windows 10 on the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Surface Pro 7</a> is as flexible as ever. It provides access to a rich ecosystem of programs and apps, and you can get them from any source you prefer, whether that be the Microsoft App Store, directly from the program&#39;s creator, or through alternative digital marketplaces. These programs are generally fully-featured versions.</p><p>Even better is the fact that <a href=\"https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2021/08/31/windows-11-available-on-october-5/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Surface Pro 7 is eligible for the upcoming Windows 11 upgrade</a>. That will make this tablet just as current as Apple&#39;s as far as operating systems are concerned. Chances are high that we&#39;ll see updates to Surface Pro 7 on the Windows 11 path for at least a few years to come.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/614e3039b414c10018625ea0?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Microsoft Surface Pro 7\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Surface Pro 7 doesn&#39;t come included with the keyboard cover, which is sold separately and adds to the cost.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><p>This puts the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">iPad Pro</a> in a more serious pinch here. The operating system is still largely more restrictive, limiting what software you can install and where you can get it from. But, the iPad app ecosystem is also fairly extensive. If there&#39;s software you want that&#39;s not available, there will likely be a fairly capable alternative.</p><p>Sometimes the apps you&#39;ll find will not offer all the same features as the desktop versions, as has been the case with some of Adobe&#39;s popular creative apps, but that list is shrinking slowly. If you&#39;re coming from macOS or Windows, you&#39;ll just want to research the specific iPadOS version of apps you need to confirm they still support all the features you rely on.</p><h2>The bottom line</h2><p>With the Surface Pro 8 finally here, Microsoft&#39;s <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.microsoft.com%2Fen-us%2Fd%2Fsurface-pro-7%2F8n17j0m5zzqs%3Factivetab%3Dpivot%3Aoverviewtab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Surface Pro 7</a> occupies a new budget space (albeit with far better performance than most budget computers) for at least the rest of 2021. It&#39;s also simply better positioned as a laptop than the iPad Pro is, using a laptop-first interface.</p><p>Meanwhile, the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fipad-pro%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">iPad Pro</a> received a serious refresh in 2021 with a great redesign, a massive upgrade to internals that will have most Ultrabooks shaking in their boots, and a display that can outshine the competition. In this match-up, the Surface Pro 7 gets a leg up on the iPad Pro as a laptop replacement with the flexibility of its Windows operating system paired with its now budget-friendly pricing.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"6086d988a3247900115896a3\" data-purchase-option=\"\">11-inch iPad Pro (2021) 00:55:28","updatedTime":"2021-09-28 00:55:28","title":"Warren Buffett used the 'Mona Lisa' to explain why art is a terrible investment - but then compared Berkshire Hathaway to an art museum","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/warren-buffett-mona-lisa-art-investment-berkshire-hathaway-national-indemnity-2021-9","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/613a1f072534ab0018537968?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Warren Buffett\" height=\"1258\" width=\"2517\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Warren Buffett.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Getty Images / Jemal Countess</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Warren Buffett dismissed art as a bad investment nearly 60 years ago.</li>\n<li>France could have made $1 quadrillion if it had invested instead of buying the Mona Lisa, he said.</li>\n<li>Buffett described investing, valuing and building businesses, and Berkshire Hathaway as art.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Warren Buffett invoked one of the most famous paintings in history to explain why art is a poor investment.</p><p>The billionaire investor tackled the topic in his 1963 letter to clients of his Buffett Partnership, the investment fund he ran before turning his attention to Berkshire Hathaway. He wanted to convey the power of compound interest in building wealth over time.</p><p>Buffett noted that Francis I, the former king of France, bought Leonardo Da Vinci&#39;s &#34;Mona Lisa&#34; in 1540 for 4,000 gold crowns, or the equivalent of $20,000. If the monarch had plowed that money into an investment generating a modest after-tax return of 6% a year, the country&#39;s coffers would be overflowing with more than $1 quadrillion by 1963, or 3,000 times its national debt, the investor pointed out.</p><p>Meanwhile, the &#34;Mona Lisa&#34; was insured at a value of $100 million in 1962, or over $900 million in today&#39;s dollars.</p><p>&#34;I trust this will end all discussion in our household about any purchase of paintings qualifying as an investment,&#34; Buffett quipped. His comments <a href=\"https://twitter.com/DividendGrowth/status/1432890602874707971\">resurfaced this month</a> courtesy of Dividend Growth Investor, a Twitter user who tweets about investing.</p><p>The famed boss of Berkshire Hathaway might not view art as a worthwhile holding, but he considers his job to be something of an art form.</p><p>&#34;Investing is the art of laying out cash now to get a whole lot more cash later on,&#34; he said at Berkshire&#39;s annual shareholder meeting in 1998. He also described valuing businesses as an &#34;art&#34; during the next year&#39;s meeting.</p><p>Moreover, Buffett has compared building a business to crafting a painting. He deployed that analogy to persuade the cofounder of National Indemnity, Jack Ringwalt, to sell his insurance company to Berkshire in 1967, he recalled at the annual meeting in 2000.</p><p>The investor asked Ringwalt if he would be happy to have a trust officer dispose of his life&#39;s work the day after he died. He reassured the entrepreneur that Berkshire would respect and not resell his business, and also allow him to continue &#34;painting&#34; it.</p><p>&#34;We won&#39;t come in and tell you to use reds instead of yellows or anything like that,&#34; Buffett recalled telling Ringwalt. &#34;So even though it&#39;s a masterpiece now, you can keep adding to it.&#34;</p><p>The Berkshire chief took the metaphor even further, framing his conglomerate as a collector of fine art.</p><p>&#34;We like to think we&#39;re the Metropolitan Museum of businesses and that we can get really outstanding creations to reside in our museum,&#34; he said.</p><p>Buffett has also described Berkshire - which owns scores of subsidiaries including Geico and See&#39;s Candies as well as multibillion-dollar stakes in Apple, Coca-Cola, and other public companies - as his magnum opus.</p><p>&#34;I regard Berkshire Hathaway sort of like a painter regards a painting, the difference being the canvas is unlimited,&#34; Buffett <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/warren-buffett-bob-woodward-microsoft-bill-gates-37-billion-deal-2020-10\">said</a> in 2016.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/warren-buffett-great-investors-traits-richer-wiser-happier-william-green-2021-9?r=US&IR=TIR=T\">&#39;Richer, Wiser, Happier&#39; author William Green interviewed dozens of the world&#39;s best investors. He breaks down the 6 key traits they share, and gives examples of them in action.</a></em></p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a says","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/stock-market-outlook-upside-surprise-ahead-sp500-analysts-cut-estimates-2021-9","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f5792abe6ff30001d4e771f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Trader NYSE green\" height=\"1000\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lucas Jackson/Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul><li><strong>An upside surprise in the stock market is brewing as Wall Street analysts cut their third-quarter S&#38;P 500 earnings estimates.</strong></li><li><strong>Analysts have cut their aggregate Q3 S&#38;P 500 earnings estimates to $48.93 per share from $49.30 per share despite seasonal data suggesting growth.</strong></li><li><strong>&#34;We can&#39;t think of a time when analysts have so seriously underestimated US corporate earnings power,&#34; DataTrek said.</strong></li><li><a href=\"https://newsletter.businessinsider.com/join/4np/10-things-opening-bell?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&#38;utm_medium=ingest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><strong>Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell</strong></a><strong>.</strong></li></ul><hr><p>An upside surprise in the stock market could take hold as Wall Street analysts cut their earnings estimates despite strong seasonal trends, DataTrek said in a Monday note.</p><p>Over the past month, third-quarter earnings estimates for the <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/index/s&p_500_500\">S&#38;P 500</a> have fallen to $48.93 per share from $49.30 per share, according to data from FactSet. That&#39;s 7% below the S&#38;P 500&#39;s actual Q2 earnings results of $52.80 per share.</p><p>The drop in S&#38;P 500 earnings estimates is surprising due to seasonal trends and recent corporate behavior, DataTrek highlighted. In economic expansions since the 1990s, Q3 earnings results are either the same or slightly higher than Q2 results. </p><p>Meanwhile, US businesses are signaling continued strength in their earnings results based on aggressive hiring trends amid a tight labor market, DataTrek said. </p><p>&#34;Would companies be hiring and advertising open positions as aggressively as the US labor market data shows if they were expecting a 7% sequential drop in profitability? It seems unlikely,&#34; DataTrek co-founder Nicholas Colas said.</p><p>And the US corporate bond market isn&#39;t signaling any stresses that would suggest a deterioration in earnings power, with low yields suggesting that cash flows should remain high and stable for years to come.</p><p>&#34;In +30 years of covering US equity markets, we can&#39;t think of a time when analysts have so seriously underestimated US corporate earnings power in any given year,&#34; Colas said. </p><p>But according to DataTrek, investors think Wall Street analysts have it wrong based on the quick recovery in recent stock market sell-offs, most recently being the <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/evergrande-stock-market-selloff-what-to-know-debt-crisis-china-2021-9\">Evergrande sell-off</a> and ensuing recovery last week.</p><p>&#34;The market thinks, rightly in our opinion, that US corporate earnings have one more leg higher versus Wall Street expectations,&#34; Colas concluded. </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a
